  DATASET
  {
    { 1100525000;;DataItem;                  ;
               DataItemTable=Table11020425;
               PrintOnlyIfDetail=Yes;
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               CompanyInfo.GET;
                               CompanyInfo.CALCFIELDS(Picture);
                               GLSetup.GET;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  Contact@1100525000 : Record 5050;
                                BEGIN
                                  CLEAR(ProjRec);
                                  IF ProjRec.GET("Project No.") THEN BEGIN
                                    ProjRec.CALCFIELDS("Principal Name", "Name Project Manager", "Name Site Manager");
                                    IF ProjPrinRec.GET("Project No.",ProjRec."Bill-to Customer No.") THEN
                                      IF CustRec.GET(ProjPrinRec.Principal) THEN
                                        FormatAddr.Customer(PrincipalAddr,CustRec);
                                    IF DimValRec.GET(GLSetup."Global Dimension 1 Code",ProjRec."Global Dimension 1 Code") THEN BEGIN
                                      IF ContactRec.GET(DimValRec."Contact No. (Company)") THEN BEGIN
                                        GobalDim1City := STRSUBSTNO('%1 %2',ContactRec.City,Text001);
                                        CompanyInfo."Name 2" := ContactRec."Name 2";
                                        CompanyInfo."Postal Address" := ContactRec.Address;
                                        CompanyInfo."Postal Post Code" := ContactRec."Post Code";
                                        CompanyInfo."Postal City" := ContactRec.City;
                                        CompanyInfo."Phone No." := ContactRec."Phone No.";
                                        CompanyInfo."Fax No." := ContactRec."Fax No.";
                                      END;
                                    END;
                                  END;

                                  IF "Approved By Name" = '' THEN
                                    IF Contact.GET("Approved By") THEN
                                      "Approved By Name" := Contact.Name;

                                  IF PrintCPAddress THEN
                                    IF "Unit Price Production Mot."."Approved By" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                      ContactRec.GET("Approved By");
                                      FormatAddr.ContactAddr(PrincipalAddr,ContactRec);
                                    END;
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=Project No.,Production Date,Code }

    { 1100525020;1;Column;ProjectNo_UnitPriceProductionMot;

    { 1100525015;1;Column;CompanyInfoBankNameCompanyInfoBankAccountNo;

    { 1000000001;1;Column;PrintOption        ;
               SourceExpr=PrintOptionInteger }

    { 1100525002;1;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table11020426;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Project No.,Project Principal,Extension Contract No.,Production Date,Code,Line No.);
               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  Contact@1100525000 : Record 5050;
                                BEGIN
                                  PrintOptionInteger := PrintOption;//0=incl. posthoeveelhied, 1=incl. vorige productie, 2=alleen productie in periode

                                  IF (PrintOption = PrintOption::"incl. posthoeveelheid") AND (Quantity = 0) THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  CALCFIELDS("Previous Production Cumulative");
                                  IF (PrintOption = PrintOption::"incl. vorige productie") AND ("Previous Production Cumulative" = 0) THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF (PrintOption = PrintOption::"alleen productie in periode") AND (Production = 0) THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;
                                END;

               DataItemLinkReference=Unit Price Production Mot.;
               DataItemLink=Project No.=FIELD(Project No.),
                            Project Principal=FIELD(Project Principal),
                            Production Date=FIELD(Production Date),
                            Code=FIELD(Code) }

  <Code>Shared Data1 as Object
Shared Data2 as Object
Shared Data3 as Object
Shared Data4 as Object

Public Function GetData(Num as Integer, Group as integer) as Object
if Group = 1 then
   Return Cstr(Choose(Num, Split(Cstr(Data1),Chr(177))))
End If

if Group = 2 then
   Return Cstr(Choose(Num, Split(Cstr(Data2),Chr(177))))
End If

if Group = 3 then
   Return Cstr(Choose(Num, Split(Cstr(Data3),Chr(177))))
End If

if Group = 4 then
   Return Cstr(Choose(Num, Split(Cstr(Data4),Chr(177))))
End If
End Function

Public Function SetData(NewData as Object,Group as integer)
  If Group = 1 and NewData &gt; "" Then
      Data1 = NewData
  End If

  If Group = 2 and NewData &gt; "" Then
      Data2 = NewData
  End If

  If Group = 3 and NewData &gt; "" Then
      Data3 = NewData
  End If

  If Group = 4 and NewData &gt; "" Then
      Data4 = NewData
  End If

  Return True
End Function

Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
